msg:The hotel shows signs that it has seen better days  despite renovations some years back.This is evident from the decor, cabinets, carpets etc in the room.which are visibly aged,.There was no central heating in the afternoon and only came on at night and in the morning when the outside temperature was around 10 degree centigrade. Despite these shortcomings, the room was clean and gives value for money for holiday makers who are not fussy about ambience and are out most of the day and return for a hot shower and sleep.The hotel location is away from the nearest town with no entertainment and eateries in the vicinity. However, it is a short walk to the entrance of the scenic park.

name:T‍r‍e‍p
info:Elegant Queen Room
info:Stayed in June 2021
info:Solo travelers
info:6 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted June 28, 2021
msg:Pretty good, great location and HOT SPRINGS!! I’m an American living in China, so I don’t try and compare with Western hotels in China. 
Hotel is pretty nice, pretty clean. Overall a good choice except 1 thing (I’ll get to it later). The breakfast was Chinese only buffet and with that in mind, very good. No coffee (I didn’t see any coffee in town either) :(
Location is good, 800m from JiuZhaiGuo a 12 way taxi ride from restaurants (******* and Chinese). 
The hot springs were very nice after a long day walking. Since earthquake and pandemic only 2 of 5 themed pools were open, but the 2 were very nice, very clean with steam room, sauna available. 
The biggie: you may have read about hot water in the room problem in other reviews. This is true and kind of a bummer. I think you need to go early if you want a warm (not hot) showers. Otherwise it’s gonna be COLD (based on my experience)

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Family-friendly Family Room
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:4 Reviews
rating:3.5
posted:Posted February 20, 2024
msg:The hotel is very big. The advantage of an old hotel is that the rooms are large, but the disadvantage is that the decoration is old.
The bedding and room hygiene were done well, and a welcome fruit plate and drinks were given.
The response speed of room service is fast and the attitude is relatively good.
The bathroom showerhead was severely clogged.
It takes ten or twenty minutes to walk from the hotel to the Mizoguchi ticket check-in area. Turn right when you exit the hotel and you will find the passenger terminal, but there are only long-distance buses.
There is only one small restaurant and a small supermarket within a 10-minute walk around the hotel. It is very deserted and all kinds of shops are vacant, making it inconvenient to travel for food and drinks.
After staying for 3 days, the hotel's hot spring was not turned on, and the hot water was not stable at night. On the morning of check-out, even the air conditioner could not blow hot air.
The hotel lobby and restaurant are very dark, and the massage chair area is the only bright place.
The breakfast at the hotel was terrible. I only ate it once and never went to that restaurant again. There is only one waiter who clears the tableware, and his communication attitude is very poor. Only the fruits for breakfast are fresh, and corn and sweet potatoes are dry and inferior products with black marks.

msg:Location: The distribution center is right outside the door, which is very convenient. It takes 15-20 minutes to walk to the Mizoguchi. There are fruit shops, Dicos, burger shops, and a few snack bars near the hotel, but there are really not many. Most of them are concentrated in Qiangu Fengqing, which is half an hour away from the hotel. You can walk out of Mizoguchi to eat and buy things. Then we took a taxi back to the hotel, which was very cheap.
Room: A 1.35-meter double bed, suitable for three people. If you are not so tall and strong, you can sleep two people in one bed. The room is quite big, and there is a large treasure pavilion, which is very friendly for storing things. There is no problem with hot water in the bathroom, sewerage is OK, and there is no peculiar smell, but it cannot be compared with hotels of the same star rating in the city. It's not hot in October, so I didn't turn on the air conditioner.
Service: The attitude of the hotel staff is very good. I don’t know if it was because of the National Day, but the hotel gave me 200ml of Yili milk on the first and second nights of my stay, two bottles every night. On the second night of my stay, I was given a plate of fruit, including small tomatoes, watermelon, and cantaloupe. I happened to have not eaten any fruit all day, so I kept the small tomatoes and continued to bring them into the ditch to satisfy my cravings on the third day (originally the 1 point redemption fruit selected on Ctrip After checking in on the first day, I checked with the front desk. Maybe this item was not shown on the Ctrip order, so I refunded the 1-point redemption. I was not sure whether the fruit plate for the next day was delivered by the hotel itself. For the guests~)
Hot spring: I was given a foot bath bucket and medicine bag on the second day, and I happened to give my mother a foot bath when I came back on the third day. There are also people taking a bath in the hot spring area outside. There are three or four small pools
Surroundings: There is a platform outside the window. Of course, it is generally impossible to climb in, except for forced climbing. The window faces the hotel parking lot. There will always be the sound of cars parking before nightfall, and there will also be a few buses. There was no sound in the middle of the night. There is a mountain view outside the window.
Breakfast: The buffet breakfast has quite a lot of varieties, basically everything is available, but again, the scale should not be compared with the same-star hotels in urban areas. After all, it is in the mountains, so the conditions are not bad.

name:T‍a‍o‍f‍u‍j‍i‍e‍r‍x‍i‍n‍g‍m‍u‍r‍o‍n‍g‍c‍h‍u‍i
info:Guestroom - Triple Occupancy
info:Stayed in April 2023
info:Family
info:5 Reviews
rating:3.5
posted:Posted May 2, 2023
msg:優點：位置特別棒。真的很靠近九寨溝景區入口，不到1公里，走路10分鐘。也許是最靠近景區的酒店之一了。特別方便。門口左右走路1-2分鐘100米左右就有小超市了。買東西也很方便。酒店旁邊就是九寨溝的旅遊集散中心。酒店工作人員還是很積極的給調換房間。
早餐還算豐盛。熱菜主食十來種吧。現煮的米線是一個特色，味道很不錯。
空調的暖風還是很給力的。


缺點：訂的是三人房，房間的衞生不是過關。淋浴間牆上還有前任留下的一根頭髮。淋浴間的浴簾是佈滿了黴斑的。
衞生間嚴重反味。第二天，酒店前台的處理到時很及時，給換了一個房間。但是依舊反味嚴重。剛進入房間的時候，因為一直開窗通風，廁所門也開着，所有沒有感覺。晚上天冷了，關了窗户打開空調。廁所的味道就無法忽略了。好像是煤氣的臭味，硫磺味，難道和温泉有關係？第一天來了就很晚了，第二天爬山累壞了，也就忍忍睡了。
三人房的位置在酒店大堂和餐廳廚房的樓上，不知道是否這這個佈局有關。普通的雙人間不知道怎麼樣。
温泉並沒有開，得過幾天等旺季的時候才會開。所有根本體會不到。訂房間的時候，並沒有特別明顯的提示。
酒店靠着集散中心，早晨大巴車很快多了起來，想睡懶覺是不太可能的了。
酒店應該是接待旅遊團比較多的。感覺散客不多。應該沒到旺季，感覺整體很冷清。或者剛營業的感覺。
可能這就是九寨溝溝口整體的水平吧。
----------------------------------------

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r

msg:最近成都疫情，到九寨溝這邊管控特別嚴，要求24小時核酸報告及綠碼才能進入。到了酒店，前台非常稱職非常負責，又檢查了一次行程碼和健康碼還有核酸證明。看得出來酒店對於疫情防控非常重視，在住過程中碰到過房間和電梯在進行消毒。公共區域有充足的洗手液和消毒液。前台辦理入住和退房都很麻利。早餐品種一般，味道還行。床品很舒服，衞生情況還行。酒店羣山圍繞，環境舒適也很清凈。酒店的地理位置非常便捷，旁邊就是客運中心，景區步行可以到達。酒店後面有邊邊街，旁邊有建設銀行。小吃，特產，超市等等也是有的，衹是比較少，可能因為疫情的原因沒怎麼開。推薦。

posted:Posted July 24, 2022
msg:看了酒店差評糾結要不要選該酒店，於是提前聯繫了攜程和酒店溝通後還是決定下單。酒店還是符合攜程五鑽標準，在硬件一般的情況下用服務彌補了。 服務一流，可以給到五星，每一個服務人員都很熱情，都主動和客人打招呼。 礦泉水兩瓶不夠喝我問阿姨多要一瓶，二話沒説看我有同伴還多給一瓶。 早餐可以，價格也算正常，如果在不提高價格的基礎上，希望你們花樣每天再多換換或許會更好。 入住和退房迅速，真心很贊。還有就是酒店位置，離景區特別近，我們是步行去的也就幾分鐘而已。至於説建議，可能硬件提升下吧，當然一提升或許價格又不一樣了。魚和熊掌不可兼得。值得推薦， 給五星好評！

msg:這酒店，我強推！ 1.位置很好，距離九寨溝溝口超近，超乎你想象的近走路幾分鐘根本不需要打車。酒店後面邊邊街有小吃和早點，每天還有當地人賣水果和當地野菌價格實惠 2.設施完備，窗簾是電動窗簾，給我升級的房間馬桶是智能的，該有都有。 3.服務好，入住前寄存行李後出去玩，也給我兩瓶水，我延遲退房，也沒有加我錢。 4.衞生好，大堂不用説，自然是非常乾淨。房間鋪的地毯，但沒有異味黴味。衞生間淋浴房洗漱台和一些角落都是乾淨的，寫字枱，衣櫃沒有灰塵。 我不是潔癖，但是會看細節，這裏住的很舒服。 網上看點評，有許多和衞生相關的評論，還有附圖，一直心有餘悸。但其實到酒店後發現評論裏的圖片和文字類容，有點言過其實了，感覺和實際有天壤之別。因為比較滿意，又續住了一晚。 勸各位，對衞生有要求的，還是推薦住這家酒店。我也會推薦後面來玩的其他朋友入住。

一樓的餐廳飯食味道一絕，價格也不貴。

msg:優勢：
1、酒店距離溝口景點檢票處大概步行10分鐘；
2、前台的男客服見我帶着倆個孩子，主動幫着拿東西並送至客房，沒有他送自己還真不一定能找到房間，裏面有點繞；
3、餐廳有個推薦油茶的姑娘，他的東西味道不錯，不甜，但好喝，100塊錢4罐。

劣勢：
1、早餐相當難吃，且沒啥可吃的；相當於7天、如家的標準；
2、入住時送了三張下午茶券，前台説是在酒店中廳用，我們等了20多分鐘根本服務員，期間叫了3次才來人，每張券可以在可樂、雪碧、橙汁中選一個，然後送一份點心，我們三張券可以選三份，結果來的男服務員説三份衹給一份點心，説是兩張券換一份，多的券不給。。。給不起就不要送券，券上寫的清楚，服務員就有權改，這男服務員就這麼牛。。。
3、酒店是幾個人合夥開的，管理也就那樣，服務員都牛成那樣，可見管理了。。。
4、入住期間趕上成都疫情再起，酒店自行加碼要求綠碼入住必須提供兩天內的核酸檢測，是不是自行加碼衹要聯繫當地12345就可知道；
5、在酒店吃了晚餐，宮保雞丁幾乎找不到雞肉，全是花生米，給餐廳提了意見，第二天點的時候雞肉是有了，但是菜量少了很多，這餐廳精打細算，估計是老闆在後廚坐陣；
